<user_name>Tour Guide</user_name>< Text>
This place is unique - it's a working horse ranch and winery, and in the same family since the 1800's. Inside the Old Fruit Shed Tasting Room you can see lots of old documents and pictures on the wall from the old days, and they have some unique gift shop items, too. Fun place to visit - you can taste wine then watch the horses in the arena getting their workout. (they also rent horses here)</Text>

< Text>
This restaurant has a big menu with lots of selections, and it seems they do the more Chinese-style dishes better than their HK-bistro-style dishes (which is fitting to their Chinese name "Cha-Chan-Teng" Ëå∂È§êÂª≥).

Although lacking "smoothness" the hot milk tea is still acceptable, but I wouldn't order the cold one again.

The Seafood Fried Rice with XO Sauce was good, with variety of seafood--even fish!--and sufficient "wok aroma" ÈëäÊ∞£, but as with the dish from any other places, one would want bigger pieces of seafood and more xo sauce.

The two Baked Rice--Baked Pork Chop and Portuguese Chicken--both lacked flavor in The sauce, left my friends and I a lot more to desire (we only finished half of each).

Service is what one gets in a typical Chinese restaurant, so you wouldn't expect much, but the restaurant itself is spacious and open, and when my friends and I stayed for a long lunch (reunion), we didn't feel pressured to leave.</Text>

I absolutely love this facility! I had a great time working there and have become passionate about working with special needs clients. 3. They lie to me when I ask for an explanation. For instance, they told me one time that they didn't pick up the packages because I had the wrong apartment number. In addition, they had already ignored 2 pickup requests the 2 days prior that had the correct apartment. Everyone there wants to blame someone else, including me. They just don't care. After my packages had been sitting outside for 3 full days (it's a miracle none were stolen) and I was overseas, I finally got ahold of someone and asked them if they could guarantee they would be picked up. They told me no, they would make no such guarantee. Guess what? They didn't pick them up, again.

4. Even when they pick up the packages, they don't scan and ship them day-of. Sometimes they take more than 24 hours to get to them all. This often means my customers wait an addition 2 days because of this branch.

5. I called the regional office and left a voicemail complaining about my local post office. At least they had a voicemail. However, they never returned my calls. There is no accountability.

I'm not sure if this office is poorly managed, poorly staffed, underfunded or some other combination of those, but I have never had a business treat a customer that gives them so much money so poorly.

Now I'm sitting with 150 packages outside my door, and I know they won't be coming to pick it up. They haven't answered the phone, and I've emailed the branch manager and several other managers and haven't gotten a response. These packages will sit for an additional 3 days because Monday is a holiday, despite working until 1am last night to make sure they were ready for pickup. What a waste of work.

I will soon have customers emailing me complaining that their coffee hasn't arrived yet. Some will cancel. Others I will give discounts to to¬†appease. I have lost thousands of dollars and no one at this post office cares.

I have never made a worse decision in my life than moving to an area controlled by this office.<//Text>< Pics>

< text>
It's a rest area. People don't come here on the basis of a review or to see the magnificent sights. They come to "rest." However, rest areas in the state are being renewed and this one was recently rebuilt. Given the choice of the gas station in Baker with the wheel for a key chain and this, this wins. They actually gave it some character and it is clean. Compared to other rest areas in the state, this deserves five stars.< /text>
